###  Petkele₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Petkele* (FIXME)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  48
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
